  <script type="text/javascript">
   $(window).load(function () {
        /* 20190225 modify header 수정 */
        
        /**-- Gnb_opener  ---**/
        var $stickyNavOffset, $windowEl = $('#window');
        if ($windowEl.length) {
            $('.gnb_opener button').on('click', function () {
                $('body').toggleClass('window');
                var $stickyNavClear = setTimeout(function () {
                    $stickyNavOffset = $('header #top_banner').outerHeight() + $('header .global-search').outerHeight();
                    stickyNavFunc($stickyNavOffset);
                    clearTimeout($stickyNavClear);
                }, 50);
            });
        } else {
            $stickyNavOffset = $('header nav').offset().top;
            stickyNavFunc($stickyNavOffset);
        }

        /**-- Sticky nav search  --**/
        $('header nav .utility li.nav_search').on('click', function () {
            TweenMax.to('#top_search.header-fixed', .4, { className: '+=active' });
        }).find('a').on('click', function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
        });

        /**-- Sticky navigation --**/
        function stickyNavFunc(offsetTop) {
            var $scrollTop = $(window).scrollTop();

            if ($scrollTop >= offsetTop) {
                $('header nav').addClass('fixed');
                $('#top_search').addClass('header-fixed');
                $('header nav .symbol, header nav .utility, #container').addClass('active');

                //window
                if ($windowEl.length) {
                    $('.gnb_opener').addClass('active');
                    $windowEl.addClass('active')
                        .find('.btn_list_open').addClass('active');
                }
            } else {
                $('header nav').removeClass('fixed');
                $('#top_search').removeClass('header-fixed');
                $('header nav .symbol, header nav .utility, #container').removeClass('active');

                //window
                if ($windowEl.length) {
                    $('.gnb_opener').removeClass('active');
                    $windowEl.removeClass('active')
                        .find('.btn_list_open').removeClass('active');
                }
            }
        }
        /* end // 20190225 modify header 수정 */

        /**-- Main top banner  --**/
        var main_bannerBtn = 0;
        $('#top_banner .btn-wrap').on('click', function () {
            if (main_bannerBtn === 0) {
                $(this).parents().find('.banner').removeClass('active');
                $(this).children('.icon.icon_up').removeClass('active')
                    .siblings('.icon.icon_down').addClass('active');
                main_bannerBtn = 1;
            } else {
                $(this).parents().find('.banner').addClass('active');
                $(this).children('.icon.icon_up').addClass('active')
                    .siblings('.icon.icon_down').removeClass('active');
                main_bannerBtn = 0;
            }
            return $stickyNavOffset = $('header nav').offset().top;
        });
        $(window).on("scroll", function () {
            stickyNavFunc($stickyNavOffset);
        });

        //와이즈 트래커 GNB 클릭 트래킹
        $('.second-nav li').on('click', function (e) {
            try {
                var trkCd = "";
                var $this = $(this);
                var $nav = $this.parents('li');
                var catlarge;
                var cateIdx;

                var $area;
                cateIdx = $nav.prevAll().length;
                catlarge = $nav.children('a').find('span').text().toUpperCase();
                catmid = "";
                $area = $this.parent().attr('class');
                switch (cateIdx) {
                    case 0:
                        if ($this.find('strong').text() == "JUST ARRIVED") {
                            trkCd = 'NEW^JUST ARRIVED';
                        }
                        else if ($area === undefined) {
                            trkCd = 'NEW^' + ($this.index() + 1) + '번상품';
                        }
                        break;
                    case 4:
                        if ($this.find('strong').text() == "SALE") {
                            trkCd = 'SALE^SALE';
                        }
                        break;
                    default:
                        if ($area == "depth3") {
                            if ($this.index() == 0) {
                                trkCd = catlarge + '^' + $this.find('strong').text();
                            } else {
                                catmid = $this.parent().children().first().find('strong').text();
                                trkCd = catlarge + '^' + catmid + '^' + $this.find('a').text();
                            }
                        }
                        else if ($area === undefined) {
                            trkCd = catlarge + '^' + ($this.index() + 1) + '번' + (catlarge == "BRAND" ? '브랜드' : '상품');
                        }
                        break;
                }
                if (trkCd != "") {
                    //_trk_flashEnvView('_TRK_CP=^GNB^' + trkCd);   // WiseTracker 제거
                }
            } catch (_e) { }
        });
    });

    function SearchKwd(kwd) {
        document.location.href = "/Search?kwd=" + encodeURI(kwd);
        return false;
    }
  </script>

    <div class="count_down_bundle ty_white" id="CountDown171032">
     <!-- 칼라 타입 ty_white -->
     <h3 class="count_down_name">
      COUNT DOWN
     </h3>
     <ul class="countdown_timer">
      <li class="time_day">
       <div class="digit">
       </div>
       <div class="label">
        Days
       </div>
      </li>
      <li class="time_hour">
       <div class="digit">
       </div>
       <div class="label">
        Hours
       </div>
      </li>
      <li class="time_min">
       <div class="digit">
       </div>
       <div class="label">
        Minutes
       </div>
      </li>
      <li class="time_sec">
       <div class="digit">
       </div>
       <div class="label">
        Seconds
       </div>
      </li>
     </ul>
    </div>
    <script type="text/javascript">
     var makeTimer171032 = setInterval(function () {
        var sectionId = "CountDown171032";

        var now = new Date(); //현재시간
        var startTime = Date.parse("2022/05/09 10:00:00");       //시작일시
        var endTime = Date.parse("2022/05/16 10:00:59") + 1000;   //종료일시 (+1초로 종료날짜 셋팅)
        var distance = endTime - (now > startTime ? now : startTime);       //시작날짜가 현재시간보다 큰 경우 Timer Start

        //Coming soon제거 (카운트다운 1초 전에 해제)
        if (now >= (startTime - 1000) && $("#" + sectionId).hasClass("st_coming_soon") === true) {
            $("#" + sectionId).removeClass("st_coming_soon");
        }

        var days = Math.floor(distance / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
        var hours = Math.floor(distance / (1000 * 60 * 60));
        var minutes = Math.floor(distance / (1000 * 60));
        var seconds = Math.floor(distance / 1000);

        var d = days < 0 ? 0 : days;
        var h = hours < 0 ? 0 : hours - (days * 24);
        var m = minutes < 0 ? 0 : minutes - (hours * 60);
        var s = seconds < 0 ? 0 : seconds - (minutes * 60);

        if (d < 1) { d = "0" + d; }
        if (h < "10") { h = "0" + h; }
        if (m < "10") { m = "0" + m; }
        if (s < "10") { s = "0" + s; }

        $("#" + sectionId + " .time_day>.digit").text(d);
        $("#" + sectionId + " .time_hour>.digit").text(h);
        $("#" + sectionId + " .time_min>.digit").text(m);
        $("#" + sectionId + " .time_sec>.digit").text(s);

        //날짜비노출 시간만으로 24시간이상 설정시
        if (days >= 1 && $("#" + sectionId + " .countdown_timer").hasClass("ty_hour_only") === true) {
            $("#" + sectionId + " .ty_hour_only > .time_hour>.digit").text(hours);
        }

        //시간을 분으로 설정 시
        if (hours >= 1 && $("#" + sectionId + " .countdown_timer").hasClass("ty_minutes_only") === true) {
            $("#" + sectionId + " .ty_minutes_only > .time_min>.digit").text(minutes);
        }

        //0 이되면 멈춤
        if (seconds < 1) {
            clearInterval(makeTimer171032);
        }
    }, 1000);
    </script>

      <!-- 시간계산코드 -->
      <script>
       $(document).ready(function () {

		var EDate = new Date(),
			EMonth = EDate.getMonth() + 1;

		if (EDate.getDate() < 10) {
		   EDay = "0"+ EDate.getDate();
		}else{
		   EDay = EDate.getDate();
		}
		if (EDate.getHours() < 10) {
		   EHours = "0"+ EDate.getHours();
		}else{
		   EHours = EDate.getHours();
		}
		if (EDate.getMinutes() < 10) {
		   EMinutes = "0"+ EDate.getMinutes();
		}else{
		   EMinutes = EDate.getMinutes();
		}
		var Eventfullday = EMonth.toString() + EDay.toString() ;
		var Efullday = parseInt(Eventfullday);
		var Etime = EHours +""+ EMinutes;

		var Edaynumber =  parseInt(Eventfullday + Etime); //정수로 표현되는 날짜와 시간(예시 10월 31일 14시 48분 => 10311448)

		var Eday_num = parseInt(Eventfullday); //정수로 표현되는 날짜
		var Etime_num = parseInt(Etime); //정수로 표현되는 시간

		$(function(){
			console.log(Edaynumber);


			if(Edaynumber < 4200000){ 
				$("#wc_coupon").hide();
			}
			else if(Edaynumber >= 4200000 && Edaynumber < 4220000){ 
				$("#wc_coupon").show();
			}
			else{
				$("#wc_coupon").hide();
			}
		});


	});
      </script>
     </div>
